Players can also build walls, which can be upgraded as a player’s town hall level increases.\r\n\r\nResources\r\nTo earn and store gold and elixir, players must build gold mines and gold storages and elixir collectors and elixir storages, respectively. Resources is used to train new troops, new defend turrets and carry out building upgrades. \r\n\r\nTroops \r\nThe game has two kinds of building for building troops, barracks to train different types of soldiers, and Army Camp to house the soldiers. Different Town hall levels are required before you can train footman, archer, gryphon, knights, paladin, siege tank and Dragons.\r\n\r\n\r\nGems\r\nAside from the game’s resources (gold, elixir), the game also uses gems as a currency.
